  <script>
    var ytpreload = ytpreload || {};
    ytpreload.SnapClassList = ['content-snap-width-1', 'content-snap-width-2',
                               'content-snap-width-3'];
    ytpreload.getSnapClass = function(guidePinned) {
      var SCROLLBAR_WIDTH = 21;
      var CONTENT_PADDING = 50;
      var GUIDE_WIDTH = 230;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_2 = 1056;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_3 = 1262;
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

      var spaceForContent = screenWidth - SCROLLBAR_WIDTH - CONTENT_PADDING;
      if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle() && guidePinned) {
        spaceForContent -= GUIDE_WIDTH;
      }

      if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_3) {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[2];
      } else if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_2){
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[1];
      } else {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[0];
      }

    };
    ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS = 'guide-pinned';
    ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS = 'show-guide';
    ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle = function() {
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;
      return screenWidth >= 1251;
    };
    (function() {
      var htmlEl = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0];
      var classList = [htmlEl.className];
        if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle()) {
          classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS);
            classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS);
        }
        classList.push(' ', ytpreload.getSnapClass(
            true));
      htmlEl.className = classList.join(' ');
    })();
  </script>

     <h2 class="intro big"> Counselors </h2> 
     <img class="centerImg header" alt="" width="582" height="247" src="/Images/header_counselors.jpg" /> 
     <div class="grid_10 prefix_1 suffix_1 alpha omega"> 
      <div class="clearfix centerTxt"> 
       <h3 class="verd intro grey" style="margin-bottom: 0;"> Help students plan, apply, get accepted, access financial aid and explore all that UC Riverside has to offer. </h3> 
       <a class="rightArrowCTA xlarge" href="/Home/FAQ">Frequently Asked Questions</a> 
      </div> 
      <hr class="style1" style="margin-bottom: 30px;" /> 
      <div class="genericBody version2 verd"> 
       <div class="grid_5 alpha"> 
        <h4> How We Stand Out</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li><a href="/WhyUCR">50 good reasons</a> to choose UCR.</li> 
         <li>See how <a href="/WhyUCR/ourRankings">we rank</a> as a UC rising star.</li> 
         <li>Explore our <a href="/Academics/collegesSchoolsMajors">colleges, schools and majors.</a></li> 
         <li>Learn about our <a href="/Academics/supportServices">special support services</a> and <a href="/Academics/honorsPrograms">honors opportunities.</a></li> 
         <li>Get to know our <a href="/Academics/faculty">faculty</a> and meet our <a href="/WhyUCR/ourStudents">students.</a></li> 
         <li>Get a feel for <a href="/CampusLife">campus life.</a></li>
        </ul> 
        <h4> How Students Get Accepted</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li> <a href="../Admissions/pathsAdmissions#incomingFreshman">Freshman Admission Requirements</a></li> 
         <li> <a href="../Admissions/pathsAdmissions#transferStudents">Transfer Admission Requirements</a></li> 
         <li> <a href="http://international.ucr.edu/HowToApply.aspx" target="_blank">International Admission Requirements</a></li> 
         <li> <a href="../Admissions/pathsAdmissions#nonTraditionalStudents">Nontraditional Admission Requirements</a></li>
        </ul> 
        <h4> How to Get Help</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Contact an <a href="/Admissions/meetCounselor">admissions counselor.</a></li> 
         <li>Access <a href="http://admission.universityofcalifornia.edu/counselors/" target="_blank">University of California information for counselors</a>. </li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
       <div class="grid_5 omega"> 
        <h4> How Students Apply </h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Guide to the <a href="/Apply">Application Process</a> </li> 
         <li>Important <a href="/Admissions/datesDeadlines">Dates and Deadlines</a></li> 
         <li><a href="/Content/PDFs/checklist_freshman.pdf">Freshman Checklist</a></li> 
         <li><a href="/Content/PDFs/checklist_transfer.pdf">Transfer Checklist</a></li> 
         <li><a href="/Content/PDFs/checklist_international_freshman.pdf">International Freshman Checklist</a></li> 
         <li><a href="/Content/PDFs/checklist_international_transfer.pdf">International Transfer Checklist</a></li> 
         <li><a href="/Content/PDFs/checklist_nontraditional.pdf">Nontraditional Student Checklist</a></li>
        </ul> 
        <h4> How Students Can Pay</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Find out <a href="/PayingForCollege/costEstimator">how affordable</a> it is to attend UCR.</li> 
         <li>See the <a href="/PayingForCollege/financialAidScholarships">many ways</a> UCR makes college possible regardless of financial challenges. </li> 
        </ul> 
        <h4> How to Stay Connected</h4> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Like us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/ucradmissions" target="_blank">Facebook</a>.</li> 
         <li>Follow us on <a href="https://twitter.com/ucradmissions" target="_blank">Twitter</a>.</li> 
         <li>Follow us on <a href="http://lifeatucr.tumblr.com/" target="_blank">Tumblr</a>.</li> 
         <li>Schedule <a href="/VisitUCR/tourOptions">a campus tour</a> or take a <a href="/VisitUCR/virtualTours">virtual tour</a> right now. </li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
      </div>

                            _prepareNodes: function() {
                                for(var cleanId in nodes){
                                    var center = Y.one("#"+cleanId+" > center");
                                    if(center != null && center && !Y.one("#" + nodes[cleanId].id)){
                                        center.set("innerHTML","");
                                        center.insert(nodes[cleanId].node);
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        };
                    })();

                    /* setting up DARLA events */
                    var w = window,
                        D = w.DARLA,
                        C = w.DARLA_CONFIG,
                        DM = w.DOC_DOMAIN_SET || 0;
                    if (D) {
                        if (D && C) {
                            C.dm = DM;
                        }
                        
                        DARLA_CONFIG.nodeMgr._prepareNodes();
                        
                        /* setting DARLA configuration */
                        DARLA.config(C);

                        /* prefetch Ads if applicable */
                        DARLA.prefetched("fc");

                        /* rendering prefetched Ad */
                        DARLA.render();  
                    }

                    return {
                        event: function (eventId, spaceId, adsSa) {
                            if (window.DARLA && eventId) {
                                DARLA_CONFIG.nodeMgr._prepareNodes();
                                var eventConfig = {};
                                if (!isNaN(spaceId)) {
                                    eventConfig.sp = spaceId;
                                }
                                /* Site attributes */
                                adsSa = (typeof adsSa !== "undefined" && adsSa !== null) ? adsSa : "";
                                eventConfig.sa = DARLA_CONFIG.events[eventId].sa_orig.replace ? DARLA_CONFIG.events[eventId].sa_orig.replace("ADSSA", adsSa) : "";
                                DARLA.event(eventId, eventConfig);
                            }
                        },
                        render: function() {
                            if (!!(Y.one('#yom-slideshow-lightbox') || Y.one('#content-lightbox') || false)) {
                                /* skip configuring DARLA in case of lightbox being triggered */
                            } else {
                                // abort current darla action
                                if (DARLA && DARLA.abort) {
                                    DARLA.abort();
                                }

                                /* prepare node is mainly for injected ad, eg. LREC within story body */
                                DARLA_CONFIG.nodeMgr._prepareNodes();

                                /* setting DARLA configuration */
                                DARLA.config(DARLA_CONFIG);

                                /* prefetch Ads if applicable */
                                DARLA.prefetched("fc");

                                /* rendering prefetched Ad */
                                DARLA.render();  
                            }
                        }
                    };

                })(); /* End of YUI.AdsDarla */

    <h2>Our Departments</h2> 
    <!-- Start Sidebar -->

       <li class="currentpage"><h3><dfn>Current page is: </dfn>Our Departments</h3></li>

     <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="title" group="Everyone" button="734" -->

     <div id="omnicontent"> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="home-image" group="Everyone" button="727" -->
      <!-- com.omniupdate.editor toolbar="IMG_ONLY" csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="700" -->
      <p><img src="/images/main/departments.jpg" alt=" " width="700" height="146" /></p>
      <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="maincontent" group="Everyone" button="707" -->
      <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="700" --> 
      <p>Learn about the departments that make up the Office of Strategic Communications.</p> 
      <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
      <div id="puzzle_indent"> 
       <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="indented" group="Everyone" button="707" -->
       <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="700" -->
       <h3><img src="/images/dept_cds.gif" alt=" " width="60" height="60" />Creative Design Services</h3> 
       <p>Serving the campus graphic arts and design needs. Visit the <a href="http://creativedesign.ucr.edu/">Creative Design Services website</a>.</p> 
       <h3><img src="/images/dept_web.gif" alt=" " width="67" height="53" />Web Development</h3> 
       <p>The Web Development team is responsible for the content, design and upkeep of the UCR online presence, including the Universitys primary UCR.EDU site. Visit the <a href="http://webdevelopment.ucr.edu/">Web Development website</a>.</p> 
       <h3><img src="/images/dept_marketing.gif" alt=" " width="62" height="53" />Marketing</h3> 
       <p>UCR Marketing is responsible for managing the universitys brand and visual identity. Our team of professionals plays a key coordinating role among all who communicate the universitys message and identity. Visit the<a href="http://marketing.ucr.edu/"> Marketing website</a>.</p> 
       <h3><img src="/images/dept_media.gif" alt=" " width="64" height="56" />Media Relations</h3> 
       <p>The UCR Office of Media Relations is responsible for interactions between the university and the media. In addition to writing and pitching press releases to media, the department produces the quarterly UCR Magazine and bi-monthly Inside UCR faculty and staff newspaper. Visit the <a href="http://mediarelations.ucr.edu/">Media Relations website</a>.</p> 
       <h3><img src="/images/dept_video.gif" alt=" " width="69" height="62" />Video Production</h3> 
       <p>The Video Production Unit documents events, produces videos for television and the internet and manages the campus studios in the basement of Sproul Hall, including the state-of-the-art Digital Communications Studio. VPU can help you tell your story visually. Visit the <a href="http://videoproduction.ucr.edu/">Video Production website</a>.</p>
       <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
      </div>

      <!-- /com.omniupdate.efp -->

    <div class="list-land" id="content"> 
     <!-- Main hero unit for a primary marketing message or call to action --> 
     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">Academic Programs and Coordination</h1> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <ul class="nav nav-tabs sub-nav tab4"> 
        <li class="active"><a class="" href="index.html">Overview</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="staff/index.html">Staff</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="academic-planning/index.html">Academic Planning</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="programs-and-initiatives/index.html">Programs &amp; Initiatives</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We support academic planning and innovation.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p><span>Academic Planning, Programs and Coordination (APPC) maintains academic policies and supports planning and analysis of instructional activities throughout the UC system. It also provides oversight and financial management of academic programs and support for new initiatives.</span></p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon staff" href="staff/index.html">Staff Directory</a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span4 blustripe"> 
       <h2 class="allCaps"> <a href="academic-planning/index.html">Accreditation &amp; program review</a> </h2> 
       <ul class="dotted-list"> 
        <li> <a href="academic-planning/accreditation.html">Accreditation procedures and resources</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="academic-planning/academic-program-review.html">Academic program review</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="academic-planning/planning-policies-and-other-activities/enrollment-planning.html">Enrollment planning</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="academic-planning/planning-policies-and-other-activities/self-supporting-programs.html">Self-supporting programs</a> </li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4 blustripe"> 
       <h2 class="allCaps"> <a href="programs-and-initiatives/index.html">Instructional programs</a> </h2> 
       <ul class="dotted-list"> 
        <li> <a href="/uconline/index.html">UC Online</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="http://www.eap.ucop.edu/Pages/default.aspx">UC Education Abroad Program (UCEAP)</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="http://www.ucdc.edu/">UC Washington Center (UCDC)</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="programs-and-initiatives/index.html">All systemwide instructional programs</a> </li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4 blustripe"> 
       <h2 class="allCaps"> <a href="programs-and-initiatives/publishing/index.html">Publishing &amp; libraries</a> </h2> 
       <ul class="dotted-list"> 
        <li> <a href="http://www.cdlib.org/">California Digital Library (CDL)</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="http://www.ucpress.edu/">UC Press</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="http://www.uctv.tv/">UCTV</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="programs-and-initiatives/publishing/index.html">All publishing programs &amp; initiatives</a> </li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row less3 novrflw"> 
      <div class="span4 grybx"> 
       <h4>Contact Us</h4> 
       <p> <br /> Academic Planning, Programs and Coordination (APPC)<br /> University of California<br /> Office of the President<br /> 1111 Franklin St., 11th floor<br /> Oakland, CA 94607<br /> </p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4 grybx"> 
       <h4>UC Online</h4> 
       <div class="flt-left">
        <a href="#"><img alt="${image.getChild('title').value}" src="/_common/files/img/fpo_uc_online_construction.jpg" /></a>
       </div> 
       <p>UC has launched a project to explore how online courses can enrich and expand academic experiences. </p> 
       <p><a href="/uconline/index.html">Learn more</a></p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4 grybx"> 
       <h4>We want your feedback</h4> 
       <p>Find a broken link? Having trouble finding something? Submit comments, questions and feedback about the new site to our web team.</p> 
       <p><a href="mailto:webeditor@ucop.edu" title="Email us">Share feedback</a></p>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
